plane-crazy 2019-01-05 01:55:09 Plane Crazy Speech:

There was a time, a much simpler time, when Plane Crazy was very inactive. It was a small game, and the community loved that. We used to build giant creations which we recreated from
famous games. We were all good at building, and one of the best was Expired. He used to build giant mechanisms which were based off of real life items. But eventually, Expired asked Mad to make water and blocks that float on water. Mad did that and everyone was happy, until Rick came along. Rick started making new updates and Mad eventually started implementing them. And now were here, all of the ogs except a few (one of those being me,) stopped playing Plane Crazy and stopped being active on the Discord server. New players have joined and they ruined the game. They praise the mods and the devs and they all ask for ranks and challenges. The game is now ruined from what happened to the game, for the purpose of this speech is to make a game of the old plane crazy for OGs only. We used to dream of new items but now we realize the horror. We need the OG community, and we need the OG Plane Crazy.
